    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1><a id="user-content-c基础入门" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#c基础入门"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>C++基础入门</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-1-c初识" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1-c初识"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1 C++初识</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-11--第一个c程序" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#11--第一个c程序"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.1  第一个C++程序</h3>
<p>编写一个C++程序总共分为4个步骤</p>
<ul>
<li>创建项目</li>
<li>创建文件</li>
<li>编写代码</li>
<li>运行程序</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-111-创建项目" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#111-创建项目"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.1.1 创建项目</h4>
<p>​	Visual Studio是我们用来编写C++程序的主要工具，我们先将它打开</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541383178746.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541383178746.png" alt="1541383178746" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541384366413.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541384366413.png" alt="1541384366413" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-112-创建文件" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#112-创建文件"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.1.2 创建文件</h4>
<p>右键源文件，选择添加-&gt;新建项</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541383817248.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541383817248.png" alt="1541383817248" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>给C++文件起个名称，然后点击添加即可。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541384140042.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541384140042.png" alt="1541384140042" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-113-编写代码" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#113-编写代码"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.1.3 编写代码</h4>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hello world<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-114-运行程序" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#114-运行程序"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.1.4 运行程序</h4>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541384818688.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541384818688.png" alt="1541384818688" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-12-注释" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#12-注释"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.2 注释</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：在代码中加一些说明和解释，方便自己或其他程序员程序员阅读代码</p>
<p><strong>两种格式</strong></p>
<ol>
<li><strong>单行注释</strong>：<code>// 描述信息</code>
<ul>
<li>通常放在一行代码的上方，或者一条语句的末尾，==对该行代码说明==</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>多行注释</strong>： <code>/* 描述信息 */</code>
<ul>
<li>通常放在一段代码的上方，==对该段代码做整体说明==</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<p>提示：编译器在编译代码时，会忽略注释的内容</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-13-变量" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#13-变量"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.3 变量</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：给一段指定的内存空间起名，方便操作这段内存</p>
<p><strong>语法</strong>：<code>数据类型 变量名 = 初始值;</code></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>变量的定义</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>语法：数据类型  变量名 = 初始值</span>

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：C++在创建变量时，必须给变量一个初始值，否则会报错</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-14--常量" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#14--常量"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.4  常量</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：用于记录程序中不可更改的数据</p>
<p>C++定义常量两种方式</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>#define</strong> 宏常量： <code>#define 常量名 常量值</code></p>
<ul>
<li>==通常在文件上方定义==，表示一个常量</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>const</strong>修饰的变量 <code>const 数据类型 常量名 = 常量值</code></p>
<ul>
<li>==通常在变量定义前加关键字const==，修饰该变量为常量，不可修改</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>1、宏常量</span>
#<span class="pl-k">define</span> <span class="pl-en">day</span> <span class="pl-c1">7</span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>一周里总共有 <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; day &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 天<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>day = 8;  //报错，宏常量不可以修改</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>2、const修饰变量</span>
	<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span> month = <span class="pl-c1">12</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>一年里总共有 <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; month &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 个月份<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>month = 24; //报错，常量是不可以修改的</span>
	
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-15-关键字" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#15-关键字"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.5 关键字</h3>
<p>**作用：**关键字是C++中预先保留的单词（标识符）</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>在定义变量或者常量时候，不要用关键字</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>C++关键字如下：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>asm</th>
<th>do</th>
<th>if</th>
<th>return</th>
<th>typedef</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>auto</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>inline</td>
<td>short</td>
<td>typeid</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bool</td>
<td>dynamic_cast</td>
<td>int</td>
<td>signed</td>
<td>typename</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>break</td>
<td>else</td>
<td>long</td>
<td>sizeof</td>
<td>union</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>case</td>
<td>enum</td>
<td>mutable</td>
<td>static</td>
<td>unsigned</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>catch</td>
<td>explicit</td>
<td>namespace</td>
<td>static_cast</td>
<td>using</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>char</td>
<td>export</td>
<td>new</td>
<td>struct</td>
<td>virtual</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>class</td>
<td>extern</td>
<td>operator</td>
<td>switch</td>
<td>void</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>const</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>private</td>
<td>template</td>
<td>volatile</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>const_cast</td>
<td>float</td>
<td>protected</td>
<td>this</td>
<td>wchar_t</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>continue</td>
<td>for</td>
<td>public</td>
<td>throw</td>
<td>while</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>default</td>
<td>friend</td>
<td>register</td>
<td>true</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>delete</td>
<td>goto</td>
<td>reinterpret_cast</td>
<td>try</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>提示：在给变量或者常量起名称时候，不要用C++得关键字，否则会产生歧义。</code></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-16-标识符命名规则" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#16-标识符命名规则"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.6 标识符命名规则</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：C++规定给标识符（变量、常量）命名时，有一套自己的规则</p>
<ul>
<li>标识符不能是关键字</li>
<li>标识符只能由字母、数字、下划线组成</li>
<li>第一个字符必须为字母或下划线</li>
<li>标识符中字母区分大小写</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>建议：给标识符命名时，争取做到见名知意的效果，方便自己和他人的阅读</p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-2-数据类型" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#2-数据类型"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2 数据类型</h2>
<p>C++规定在创建一个变量或者常量时，必须要指定出相应的数据类型，否则无法给变量分配内存</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-21-整型" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#21-整型"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.1 整型</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：整型变量表示的是==整数类型==的数据</p>
<p>C++中能够表示整型的类型有以下几种方式，<strong>区别在于所占内存空间不同</strong>：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>数据类型</strong></th>
<th><strong>占用空间</strong></th>
<th>取值范围</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>short(短整型)</td>
<td>2字节</td>
<td>(-2^15 ~ 2^15-1)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>int(整型)</td>
<td>4字节</td>
<td>(-2^31 ~ 2^31-1)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>long(长整形)</td>
<td>Windows为4字节，Linux为4字节(32位)，8字节(64位)</td>
<td>(-2^31 ~ 2^31-1)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>long long(长长整形)</td>
<td>8字节</td>
<td>(-2^63 ~ 2^63-1)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3><a id="user-content-22-sizeof关键字" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#22-sizeof关键字"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.2 sizeof关键字</h3>
<p>**作用：**利用sizeof关键字可以==统计数据类型所占内存大小==</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong> <code>sizeof( 数据类型 / 变量)</code></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>short 类型所占内存空间为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">short</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>int 类型所占内存空间为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>long 类型所占内存空间为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">long</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>long long 类型所占内存空间为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">long</span> <span class="pl-k">long</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>整型结论</strong>：==short &lt; int &lt;= long &lt;= long long==</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-23-实型浮点型" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#23-实型浮点型"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.3 实型（浮点型）</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：用于==表示小数==</p>
<p>浮点型变量分为两种：</p>
<ol>
<li>单精度float</li>
<li>双精度double</li>
</ol>
<p>两者的<strong>区别</strong>在于表示的有效数字范围不同。</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>数据类型</strong></th>
<th><strong>占用空间</strong></th>
<th><strong>有效数字范围</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>float</td>
<td>4字节</td>
<td>7位有效数字</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>double</td>
<td>8字节</td>
<td>15～16位有效数字</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">float</span> f1 = <span class="pl-c1">3</span>.<span class="pl-c1">14f</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">double</span> d1 = <span class="pl-c1">3.14</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; f1 &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; d1&lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>float  sizeof = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(f1) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>double sizeof = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(d1) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>科学计数法</span>
	<span class="pl-k">float</span> f2 = <span class="pl-c1">3e2</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 3 * 10 ^ 2 </span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>f2 = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; f2 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">float</span> f3 = <span class="pl-c1">3e-2</span>;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 3 * 0.1 ^ 2</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>f3 = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; f3 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-24-字符型" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#24-字符型"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.4 字符型</h3>
<p>**作用：**字符型变量用于显示单个字符</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code>char ch = 'a';</code></p>
<blockquote>
<p>注意1：在显示字符型变量时，用单引号将字符括起来，不要用双引号</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>注意2：单引号内只能有一个字符，不可以是字符串</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>C和C++中字符型变量只占用==1个字节==。</li>
<li>字符型变量并不是把字符本身放到内存中存储，而是将对应的ASCII编码放入到存储单元</li>
</ul>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	
	<span class="pl-k">char</span> ch = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; ch &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">char</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>ch = "abcde"; //错误，不可以用双引号</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>ch = 'abcde'; //错误，单引号内只能引用一个字符</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; (<span class="pl-k">int</span>)ch &lt;&lt; endl;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>查看字符a对应的ASCII码</span>
	ch = <span class="pl-c1">97</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>可以直接用ASCII给字符型变量赋值</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; ch &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>

<p>ASCII 码大致由以下<strong>两部分组</strong>成：</p>
<ul>
<li>ASCII 非打印控制字符： ASCII 表上的数字 <strong>0-31</strong> 分配给了控制字符，用于控制像打印机等一些外围设备。</li>
<li>ASCII 打印字符：数字 <strong>32-126</strong> 分配给了能在键盘上找到的字符，当查看或打印文档时就会出现。</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-25-转义字符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#25-转义字符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.5 转义字符</h3>
<p>**作用：**用于表示一些==不能显示出来的ASCII字符==</p>
<p>现阶段我们常用的转义字符有：<code> \n  \\  \t</code></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>转义字符</strong></th>
<th><strong>含义</strong></th>
<th><strong>ASCII</strong>码值（十进制）</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>\a</td>
<td>警报</td>
<td>007</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\b</td>
<td>退格(BS) ，将当前位置移到前一列</td>
<td>008</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\f</td>
<td>换页(FF)，将当前位置移到下页开头</td>
<td>012</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>\n</strong></td>
<td><strong>换行(LF) ，将当前位置移到下一行开头</strong></td>
<td><strong>010</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\r</td>
<td>回车(CR) ，将当前位置移到本行开头</td>
<td>013</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>\t</strong></td>
<td><strong>水平制表(HT)  （跳到下一个TAB位置）</strong></td>
<td><strong>009</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\v</td>
<td>垂直制表(VT)</td>
<td>011</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>\\</strong></td>
<td><strong>代表一个反斜线字符""</strong></td>
<td><strong>092</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>'</td>
<td>代表一个单引号（撇号）字符</td>
<td>039</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"</td>
<td>代表一个双引号字符</td>
<td>034</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>?</td>
<td>代表一个问号</td>
<td>063</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\0</td>
<td>数字0</td>
<td>000</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\ddd</td>
<td>8进制转义字符，d范围0~7</td>
<td>3位8进制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>\xhh</td>
<td>16进制转义字符，h范围0<del>9，a</del>f，A~F</td>
<td>3位16进制</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	
	
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\\</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\t</span>Hello<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-26-字符串型" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#26-字符串型"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.6 字符串型</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：用于表示一串字符</p>
<p><strong>两种风格</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>C风格字符串</strong>： <code>char 变量名[] = "字符串值"</code></p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">char</span> str1[] = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>hello world<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; str1 &lt;&lt; endl;
    
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：C风格的字符串要用双引号括起来</p>
</blockquote>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>C++风格字符串</strong>：  <code>string  变量名 = "字符串值"</code></p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	string str = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>hello world<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; str &lt;&lt; endl;
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p>​</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：C++风格字符串，需要加入头文件==#include&lt;string&gt;==</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-27-布尔类型-bool" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#27-布尔类型-bool"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.7 布尔类型 bool</h3>
<p>**作用：**布尔数据类型代表真或假的值</p>
<p>bool类型只有两个值：</p>
<ul>
<li>true  --- 真（本质是1）</li>
<li>false --- 假（本质是0）</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>bool类型占==1个字节==大小</strong></p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">bool</span> flag = <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; flag &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>

	flag = <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; flag &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>size of bool = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">bool</span>) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>1</span>
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-28-数据的输入" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#28-数据的输入"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.8 数据的输入</h3>
<p><strong>作用：用于从键盘获取数据</strong></p>
<p>**关键字：**cin</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong> <code>cin &gt;&gt; 变量 </code></p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(){

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>整型输入</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入整型变量：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; a;
	cout &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>浮点型输入</span>
	<span class="pl-k">double</span> d = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入浮点型变量：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; d;
	cout &lt;&lt; d &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>字符型输入</span>
	<span class="pl-k">char</span> ch = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入字符型变量：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; ch;
	cout &lt;&lt; ch &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>字符串型输入</span>
	string str;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入字符串型变量：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; str;
	cout &lt;&lt; str &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>布尔类型输入</span>
	<span class="pl-k">bool</span> flag = <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入布尔型变量：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; flag;
	cout &lt;&lt; flag &lt;&lt; endl;
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
	<span class="pl-k">return</span> EXIT_SUCCESS;
}</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-3-运算符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#3-运算符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3 运算符</h2>
<p>**作用：**用于执行代码的运算</p>
<p>本章我们主要讲解以下几类运算符：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>运算符类型</strong></th>
<th><strong>作用</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>算术运算符</td>
<td>用于处理四则运算</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>赋值运算符</td>
<td>用于将表达式的值赋给变量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>比较运算符</td>
<td>用于表达式的比较，并返回一个真值或假值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>逻辑运算符</td>
<td>用于根据表达式的值返回真值或假值</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3><a id="user-content-31-算术运算符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#31-算术运算符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3.1 算术运算符</h3>
<p><strong>作用</strong>：用于处理四则运算</p>
<p>算术运算符包括以下符号：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>运算符</strong></th>
<th><strong>术语</strong></th>
<th><strong>示例</strong></th>
<th><strong>结果</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>+</td>
<td>正号</td>
<td>+3</td>
<td>3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-</td>
<td>负号</td>
<td>-3</td>
<td>-3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>+</td>
<td>加</td>
<td>10 + 5</td>
<td>15</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-</td>
<td>减</td>
<td>10 - 5</td>
<td>5</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>*</td>
<td>乘</td>
<td>10 * 5</td>
<td>50</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>/</td>
<td>除</td>
<td>10 / 5</td>
<td>2</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>%</td>
<td>取模(取余)</td>
<td>10 % 3</td>
<td>1</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>++</td>
<td>前置递增</td>
<td>a=2; b=++a;</td>
<td>a=3; b=3;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>++</td>
<td>后置递增</td>
<td>a=2; b=a++;</td>
<td>a=3; b=2;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>--</td>
<td>前置递减</td>
<td>a=2; b=--a;</td>
<td>a=1; b=1;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>--</td>
<td>后置递减</td>
<td>a=2; b=a--;</td>
<td>a=1; b=2;</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>示例1：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>加减乘除</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a1 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b1 = <span class="pl-c1">3</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; a1 + b1 &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; a1 - b1 &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; a1 * b1 &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; a1 / b1 &lt;&lt; endl;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>两个整数相除结果依然是整数</span>

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a2 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b2 = <span class="pl-c1">20</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; a2 / b2 &lt;&lt; endl; 

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a3 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b3 = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>cout &lt;&lt; a3 / b3 &lt;&lt; endl; //报错，除数不可以为0</span>


	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>两个小数可以相除</span>
	<span class="pl-k">double</span> d1 = <span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">double</span> d2 = <span class="pl-c1">0.25</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; d1 / d2 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：在除法运算中，除数不能为0</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>示例2：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>取模</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a1 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b1 = <span class="pl-c1">3</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span> % <span class="pl-c1">3</span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a2 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b2 = <span class="pl-c1">20</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; a2 % b2 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a3 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b3 = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>cout &lt;&lt; a3 % b3 &lt;&lt; endl; //取模运算时，除数也不能为0</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>两个小数不可以取模</span>
	<span class="pl-k">double</span> d1 = <span class="pl-c1">3.14</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">double</span> d2 = <span class="pl-c1">1.1</span>;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>cout &lt;&lt; d1 % d2 &lt;&lt; endl;</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}
</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：只有整型变量可以进行取模运算</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>示例3：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>递增</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>后置递增</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a++; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>等价于a = a + 1</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 11</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>前置递增</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	++b;
	cout &lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 11</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>区别</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>前置递增先对变量进行++，再计算表达式</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a2 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b2 = ++a2 * <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; b2 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>后置递增先计算表达式，后对变量进行++</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a3 = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b3 = a3++ * <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; b3 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}
</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：前置递增先对变量进行++，再计算表达式，后置递增相反</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-32-赋值运算符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#32-赋值运算符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3.2 赋值运算符</h3>
<p>**作用：**用于将表达式的值赋给变量</p>
<p>赋值运算符包括以下几个符号：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>运算符</strong></th>
<th><strong>术语</strong></th>
<th><strong>示例</strong></th>
<th><strong>结果</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>=</td>
<td>赋值</td>
<td>a=2; b=3;</td>
<td>a=2; b=3;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>+=</td>
<td>加等于</td>
<td>a=0; a+=2;</td>
<td>a=2;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-=</td>
<td>减等于</td>
<td>a=5; a-=3;</td>
<td>a=2;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>*=</td>
<td>乘等于</td>
<td>a=2; a*=2;</td>
<td>a=4;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>/=</td>
<td>除等于</td>
<td>a=4; a/=2;</td>
<td>a=2;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>%=</td>
<td>模等于</td>
<td>a=3; a%2;</td>
<td>a=1;</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>赋值运算符</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> =</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> +=</span>
	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a += <span class="pl-c1">2</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> a = a + 2;</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> -=</span>
	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a -= <span class="pl-c1">2</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> a = a - 2</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> *=</span>
	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a *= <span class="pl-c1">2</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> a = a * 2</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> /=</span>
	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a /= <span class="pl-c1">2</span>;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> a = a / 2;</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> %=</span>
	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	a %= <span class="pl-c1">2</span>;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> a = a % 2;</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-33-比较运算符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#33-比较运算符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3.3 比较运算符</h3>
<p>**作用：**用于表达式的比较，并返回一个真值或假值</p>
<p>比较运算符有以下符号：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>运算符</strong></th>
<th><strong>术语</strong></th>
<th><strong>示例</strong></th>
<th><strong>结果</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>==</td>
<td>相等于</td>
<td>4 == 3</td>
<td>0</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>!=</td>
<td>不等于</td>
<td>4 != 3</td>
<td>1</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>&lt;</td>
<td>小于</td>
<td>4 &lt; 3</td>
<td>0</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>&gt;</td>
<td>大于</td>
<td>4 &gt; 3</td>
<td>1</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>&lt;=</td>
<td>小于等于</td>
<td>4 &lt;= 3</td>
<td>0</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>&gt;=</td>
<td>大于等于</td>
<td>4 &gt;= 1</td>
<td>1</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">20</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a == b) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0 </span>

	cout &lt;&lt; (a != b) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &gt; b) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &lt; b) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &gt;= b) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &lt;= b) &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：C和C++ 语言的比较运算中， ==“真”用数字“1”来表示， “假”用数字“0”来表示。==</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-34-逻辑运算符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#34-逻辑运算符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3.4 逻辑运算符</h3>
<p>**作用：**用于根据表达式的值返回真值或假值</p>
<p>逻辑运算符有以下符号：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>运算符</strong></th>
<th><strong>术语</strong></th>
<th><strong>示例</strong></th>
<th><strong>结果</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>!</td>
<td>非</td>
<td>!a</td>
<td>如果a为假，则!a为真；  如果a为真，则!a为假。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>&amp;&amp;</td>
<td>与</td>
<td>a &amp;&amp; b</td>
<td>如果a和b都为真，则结果为真，否则为假。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>||</td>
<td>或</td>
<td>a || b</td>
<td>如果a和b有一个为真，则结果为真，二者都为假时，结果为假。</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>**示例1：**逻辑非</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>逻辑运算符  --- 非</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; !a &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; !!a &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结： 真变假，假变真</p>
</blockquote>
<p>**示例2：**逻辑与</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>逻辑运算符  --- 与</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &amp;&amp; b) &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>

	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	b = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &amp;&amp; b) &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0 </span>

	a = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	b = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a &amp;&amp; b) &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}
</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：逻辑==与==运算符总结： ==同真为真，其余为假==</p>
</blockquote>
<p>**示例3：**逻辑或</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>逻辑运算符  --- 或</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a || b) &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1</span>

	a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	b = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a || b) &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 1 </span>

	a = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	b = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; (a || b) &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 0</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>逻辑==或==运算符总结： ==同假为假，其余为真==</p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-4-程序流程结构" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#4-程序流程结构"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4 程序流程结构</h2>
<p>C/C++支持最基本的三种程序运行结构：==顺序结构、选择结构、循环结构==</p>
<ul>
<li>顺序结构：程序按顺序执行，不发生跳转</li>
<li>选择结构：依据条件是否满足，有选择的执行相应功能</li>
<li>循环结构：依据条件是否满足，循环多次执行某段代码</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-41-选择结构" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#41-选择结构"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.1 选择结构</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-411-if语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#411-if语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.1.1 if语句</h4>
<p>**作用：**执行满足条件的语句</p>
<p>if语句的三种形式</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>单行格式if语句</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>多行格式if语句</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>多条件的if语句</p>
<p>​</p>
</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>
<p>单行格式if语句：<code>if(条件){ 条件满足执行的语句 }</code></p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002.png" alt="img" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>选择结构-单行if语句</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>输入一个分数，如果分数大于600分，视为考上一本大学，并在屏幕上打印</span>

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入一个分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; score;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>您输入的分数为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; score &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>if语句</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>注意事项，在if判断语句后面，不要加分号</span>
	<span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">600</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了一本大学！！！<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p>​</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：if条件表达式后不要加分号</p>
</blockquote>
<ol start="2">
<li>多行格式if语句：<code>if(条件){ 条件满足执行的语句 }else{ 条件不满足执行的语句 };</code></li>
</ol>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541662519170.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541662519170.png" alt="img" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>​</p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入考试分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	cin &gt;&gt; score;

	<span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">600</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了一本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span>
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我未考上一本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<ol start="3">
<li>多条件的if语句：<code>if(条件1){ 条件1满足执行的语句 }else if(条件2){条件2满足执行的语句}... else{ 都不满足执行的语句}</code></li>
</ol>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541662566808.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541662566808.png" alt="img" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>​</p>
<p>​</p>
<p>​</p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>	<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入考试分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	cin &gt;&gt; score;

	<span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">600</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了一本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">500</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了二本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">400</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了三本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span>
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我未考上本科<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p>​</p>
<p><strong>嵌套if语句</strong>：在if语句中，可以嵌套使用if语句，达到更精确的条件判断</p>
<p>案例需求：</p>
<ul>
<li>提示用户输入一个高考考试分数，根据分数做如下判断</li>
<li>分数如果大于600分视为考上一本，大于500分考上二本，大于400考上三本，其余视为未考上本科；</li>
<li>在一本分数中，如果大于700分，考入北大，大于650分，考入清华，大于600考入人大。</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请输入考试分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	cin &gt;&gt; score;

	<span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">600</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了一本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">700</span>)
		{
			cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了北大<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		}
		<span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">650</span>)
		{
			cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了清华<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		}
		<span class="pl-k">else</span>
		{
			cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了人大<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		}
		
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">500</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了二本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (score &gt; <span class="pl-c1">400</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我考上了三本大学<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	<span class="pl-k">else</span>
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>我未考上本科<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p><strong>练习案例：</strong> 三只小猪称体重</p>
<p>有三只小猪ABC，请分别输入三只小猪的体重，并且判断哪只小猪最重？<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/%E4%B8%89%E5%8F%AA%E5%B0%8F%E7%8C%AA.jpg"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/%E4%B8%89%E5%8F%AA%E5%B0%8F%E7%8C%AA.jpg" alt="三只小猪" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-412-三目运算符" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#412-三目运算符"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.1.2 三目运算符</h4>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 通过三目运算符实现简单的判断</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code>表达式1 ? 表达式2 ：表达式3</code></p>
<p><strong>解释：</strong></p>
<p>如果表达式1的值为真，执行表达式2，并返回表达式2的结果；</p>
<p>如果表达式1的值为假，执行表达式3，并返回表达式3的结果。</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">20</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> c = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	c = a &gt; b ? a : b;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; c &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>C++中三目运算符返回的是变量,可以继续赋值</span>

	(a &gt; b ? a : b) = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>b = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; c &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：和if语句比较，三目运算符优点是短小整洁，缺点是如果用嵌套，结构不清晰</p>
</blockquote>
<h4><a id="user-content-413-switch语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#413-switch语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.1.3 switch语句</h4>
<p>**作用：**执行多条件分支语句</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">switch</span>(表达式)

{

	<span class="pl-k">case</span> 结果<span class="pl-c1">1</span>：执行语句;<span class="pl-k">break</span>;

	<span class="pl-k">case</span> 结果<span class="pl-c1">2</span>：执行语句;<span class="pl-k">break</span>;

	...

	<span class="pl-k">default</span>:执行语句;<span class="pl-k">break</span>;

}
</pre></div>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>请给电影评分 </span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>10 ~ 9   经典   </span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 8 ~ 7   非常好</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 6 ~ 5   一般</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 5分以下 烂片</span>

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请给电影打分<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cin &gt;&gt; score;

	<span class="pl-k">switch</span> (score)
	{
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>:
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">9</span>:
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>经典<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">8</span>:
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>非常好<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">7</span>:
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">6</span>:
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>一般<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">default</span>:
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>烂片<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意1：switch语句中表达式类型只能是整型或者字符型</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>注意2：case里如果没有break，那么程序会一直向下执行</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：与if语句比，对于多条件判断时，switch的结构清晰，执行效率高，缺点是switch不可以判断区间</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-42-循环结构" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#42-循环结构"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.2 循环结构</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-421-while循环语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#421-while循环语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.2.1 while循环语句</h4>
<p>**作用：**满足循环条件，执行循环语句</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code> while(循环条件){ 循环语句 }</code></p>
<p><strong>解释：</strong>==只要循环条件的结果为真，就执行循环语句==</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541668640382.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541668640382.png" alt="img" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> num = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">while</span> (num &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>num = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; num &lt;&lt; endl;
		num++;
	}
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：在执行循环语句时候，程序必须提供跳出循环的出口，否则出现死循环</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>while循环练习案例：</strong>==猜数字==</p>
<p>**案例描述：**系统随机生成一个1到100之间的数字，玩家进行猜测，如果猜错，提示玩家数字过大或过小，如果猜对恭喜玩家胜利，并且退出游戏。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/%E7%8C%9C%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%97.jpg"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/%E7%8C%9C%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%97.jpg" alt="猜数字" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-422-dowhile循环语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#422-dowhile循环语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.2.2 do...while循环语句</h4>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 满足循环条件，执行循环语句</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong> <code>do{ 循环语句 } while(循环条件);</code></p>
<p>**注意：**与while的区别在于==do...while会先执行一次循环语句==，再判断循环条件</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541671163478.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/clip_image002-1541671163478.png" alt="img" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> num = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	<span class="pl-k">do</span>
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; num &lt;&lt; endl;
		num++;

	} <span class="pl-k">while</span> (num &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>);
	
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：与while循环区别在于，do...while先执行一次循环语句，再判断循环条件</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>练习案例：水仙花数</strong></p>
<p>**案例描述：**水仙花数是指一个 3 位数，它的每个位上的数字的 3次幂之和等于它本身</p>
<p>例如：1^3 + 5^3+ 3^3 = 153</p>
<p>请利用do...while语句，求出所有3位数中的水仙花数</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-423-for循环语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#423-for循环语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.2.3 for循环语句</h4>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 满足循环条件，执行循环语句</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code> for(起始表达式;条件表达式;末尾循环体) { 循环语句; }</code></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; i &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p><strong>详解：</strong></p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541673704101.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541673704101.png" alt="1541673704101" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：for循环中的表达式，要用分号进行分隔</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：while , do...while, for都是开发中常用的循环语句，for循环结构比较清晰，比较常用</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>练习案例：敲桌子</strong></p>
<p>案例描述：从1开始数到数字100， 如果数字个位含有7，或者数字十位含有7，或者该数字是7的倍数，我们打印敲桌子，其余数字直接打印输出。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/timg.gif"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/timg.gif" alt="timg" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-424-嵌套循环" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#424-嵌套循环"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.2.4 嵌套循环</h4>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 在循环体中再嵌套一层循环，解决一些实际问题</p>
<p>例如我们想在屏幕中打印如下图片，就需要利用嵌套循环</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541676003486.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541676003486.png" alt="1541676003486" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>外层循环执行1次，内层循环执行1轮</span>
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; j++)
		{
			cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>*<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
		}
		cout &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p>**练习案例：**乘法口诀表</p>
<p>案例描述：利用嵌套循环，实现九九乘法表</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/0006018857256120_b.jpg"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/0006018857256120_b.jpg" alt="0006018857256120_b" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-43-跳转语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#43-跳转语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.3 跳转语句</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-431-break语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#431-break语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.3.1 break语句</h4>
<p><strong>作用:</strong> 用于跳出==选择结构==或者==循环结构==</p>
<p>break使用的时机：</p>
<ul>
<li>出现在switch条件语句中，作用是终止case并跳出switch</li>
<li>出现在循环语句中，作用是跳出当前的循环语句</li>
<li>出现在嵌套循环中，跳出最近的内层循环语句</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例1：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>1、在switch 语句中使用break</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>请选择您挑战副本的难度：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1、普通<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2、中等<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3、困难<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> num = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;

	cin &gt;&gt; num;

	<span class="pl-k">switch</span> (num)
	{
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>:
