		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>您选择的是普通难度<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>:
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>您选择的是中等难度<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>:
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>您选择的是困难难度<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p><strong>示例2：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>2、在循环语句中用break</span>
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">if</span> (i == <span class="pl-c1">5</span>)
		{
			<span class="pl-k">break</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>跳出循环语句</span>
		}
		cout &lt;&lt; i &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p><strong>示例3：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>在嵌套循环语句中使用break，退出内层循环</span>
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; j++)
		{
			<span class="pl-k">if</span> (j == <span class="pl-c1">5</span>)
			{
				<span class="pl-k">break</span>;
			}
			cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>*<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
		}
		cout &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-432-continue语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#432-continue语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.3.2 continue语句</h4>
<p>**作用：**在==循环语句==中，跳过本次循环中余下尚未执行的语句，继续执行下一次循环</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">100</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">if</span> (i % <span class="pl-c1">2</span> == <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
		{
			<span class="pl-k">continue</span>;
		}
		cout &lt;&lt; i &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：continue并没有使整个循环终止，而break会跳出循环</p>
</blockquote>
<h4><a id="user-content-433-goto语句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#433-goto语句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.3.3 goto语句</h4>
<p>**作用：**可以无条件跳转语句</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong> <code>goto 标记;</code></p>
<p>**解释：**如果标记的名称存在，执行到goto语句时，会跳转到标记的位置</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">goto</span> FLAG;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	FLAG:

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>5<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：在程序中不建议使用goto语句，以免造成程序流程混乱</p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-5-数组" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#5-数组"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5 数组</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-51-概述" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#51-概述"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.1 概述</h3>
<p>所谓数组，就是一个集合，里面存放了相同类型的数据元素</p>
<p>**特点1：**数组中的每个==数据元素都是相同的数据类型==</p>
<p>**特点2：**数组是由==连续的内存==位置组成的</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541748375356.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541748375356.png" alt="1541748375356" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-52-一维数组" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#52-一维数组"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.2 一维数组</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-521-一维数组定义方式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#521-一维数组定义方式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.2.1 一维数组定义方式</h4>
<p>一维数组定义的三种方式：</p>
<ol>
<li><code>数据类型  数组名[ 数组长度 ];</code></li>
<li><code>数据类型  数组名[ 数组长度 ] = { 值1，值2 ...};</code></li>
<li><code>数据类型  数组名[ ] = { 值1，值2 ...};</code></li>
</ol>
<p>示例</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>定义方式1</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数据类型 数组名[元素个数];</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score[<span class="pl-c1">10</span>];

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>利用下标赋值</span>
	score[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
	score[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">99</span>;
	score[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">85</span>;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>利用下标输出</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; score[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; score[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; score[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;


	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>第二种定义方式</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数据类型 数组名[元素个数] =  {值1，值2 ，值3 ...};</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>如果{}内不足10个数据，剩余数据用0补全</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score2[<span class="pl-c1">10</span>] = { <span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">90</span>,<span class="pl-c1">80</span>,<span class="pl-c1">70</span>,<span class="pl-c1">60</span>,<span class="pl-c1">50</span>,<span class="pl-c1">40</span>,<span class="pl-c1">30</span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span> };
	
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>逐个输出</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>cout &lt;&lt; score2[0] &lt;&lt; endl;</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>cout &lt;&lt; score2[1] &lt;&lt; endl;</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>一个一个输出太麻烦，因此可以利用循环进行输出</span>
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; score2[i] &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>定义方式3</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数据类型 数组名[] =  {值1，值2 ，值3 ...};</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score3[] = { <span class="pl-c1">100</span>,<span class="pl-c1">90</span>,<span class="pl-c1">80</span>,<span class="pl-c1">70</span>,<span class="pl-c1">60</span>,<span class="pl-c1">50</span>,<span class="pl-c1">40</span>,<span class="pl-c1">30</span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span> };

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; score3[i] &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结1：数组名的命名规范与变量名命名规范一致，不要和变量重名</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结2：数组中下标是从0开始索引</p>
</blockquote>
<h4><a id="user-content-522-一维数组数组名" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#522-一维数组数组名"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.2.2 一维数组数组名</h4>
<p>一维数组名称的<strong>用途</strong>：</p>
<ol>
<li>可以统计整个数组在内存中的长度</li>
<li>可以获取数组在内存中的首地址</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数组名用途</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>1、可以获取整个数组占用内存空间大小</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">10</span>] = { <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span>,<span class="pl-c1">7</span>,<span class="pl-c1">8</span>,<span class="pl-c1">9</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span> };

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>整个数组所占内存空间为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>每个元素所占内存空间为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>数组的元素个数为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr) / <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>2、可以通过数组名获取到数组首地址</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>数组首地址为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; (<span class="pl-k">int</span>)arr &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>数组中第一个元素地址为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; (<span class="pl-k">int</span>)&amp;arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>数组中第二个元素地址为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; (<span class="pl-k">int</span>)&amp;arr[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>arr = 100; 错误，数组名是常量，因此不可以赋值</span>


	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：数组名是常量，不可以赋值</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结1：直接打印数组名，可以查看数组所占内存的首地址</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结2：对数组名进行sizeof，可以获取整个数组占内存空间的大小</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>练习案例1</strong>：五只小猪称体重</p>
<p><strong>案例描述：</strong></p>
<p>在一个数组中记录了五只小猪的体重，如：int arr[5] = {300,350,200,400,250};</p>
<p>找出并打印最重的小猪体重。</p>
<p>**练习案例2：**数组元素逆置</p>
<p>**案例描述：**请声明一个5个元素的数组，并且将元素逆置.</p>
<p>(如原数组元素为：1,3,2,5,4;逆置后输出结果为:4,5,2,3,1);</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-523-冒泡排序" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#523-冒泡排序"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.2.3 冒泡排序</h4>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 最常用的排序算法，对数组内元素进行排序</p>
<ol>
<li>比较相邻的元素。如果第一个比第二个大，就交换他们两个。</li>
<li>对每一对相邻元素做同样的工作，执行完毕后，找到第一个最大值。</li>
<li>重复以上的步骤，每次比较次数-1，直到不需要比较</li>
</ol>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541905327273.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541905327273.png" alt="1541905327273" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong> 将数组 { 4,2,8,0,5,7,1,3,9 } 进行升序排序</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">9</span>] = { <span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">8</span>,<span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">7</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">9</span> };

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">9</span> - <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">9</span> - <span class="pl-c1">1</span> - i; j++)
		{
			<span class="pl-k">if</span> (arr[j] &gt; arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>])
			{
				<span class="pl-k">int</span> temp = arr[j];
				arr[j] = arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>];
				arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>] = temp;
			}
		}
	}

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">9</span>; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; arr[i] &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
    
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-53-二维数组" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#53-二维数组"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.3 二维数组</h3>
<p>二维数组就是在一维数组上，多加一个维度。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/blob/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541905559138.png"><img src="/AnkerLeng/Cpp-0-1-Resource/raw/master/%E7%AC%AC1%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5C%2B%2B%20%E5%8C%A0%E5%BF%83%E4%B9%8B%E4%BD%9C%20%E4%BB%8E0%E5%88%B01%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8/C%2B%2B%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%B2%E4%B9%89/assets/1541905559138.png" alt="1541905559138" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-531-二维数组定义方式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#531-二维数组定义方式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.3.1 二维数组定义方式</h4>
<p>二维数组定义的四种方式：</p>
<ol>
<li><code>数据类型  数组名[ 行数 ][ 列数 ];</code></li>
<li><code>数据类型  数组名[ 行数 ][ 列数 ] = { {数据1，数据2 } ，{数据3，数据4 } };</code></li>
<li><code>数据类型  数组名[ 行数 ][ 列数 ] = { 数据1，数据2，数据3，数据4};</code></li>
<li><code> 数据类型  数组名[  ][ 列数 ] = { 数据1，数据2，数据3，数据4};</code></li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<p>建议：以上4种定义方式，利用==第二种更加直观，提高代码的可读性==</p>
</blockquote>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>方式1  </span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数组类型 数组名 [行数][列数]</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>][<span class="pl-c1">3</span>];
	arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
	arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">2</span>;
	arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">2</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">3</span>;
	arr[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>][<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">4</span>;
	arr[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>][<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">5</span>;
	arr[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>][<span class="pl-c1">2</span>] = <span class="pl-c1">6</span>;

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">2</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">3</span>; j++)
		{
			cout &lt;&lt; arr[i][j] &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
		}
		cout &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>方式2 </span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数据类型 数组名[行数][列数] = { {数据1，数据2 } ，{数据3，数据4 } };</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr2[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>][<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] =
	{
		{<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>},
		{<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span>}
	};

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>方式3</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数据类型 数组名[行数][列数] = { 数据1，数据2 ,数据3，数据4  };</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr3[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>][<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] = { <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span> }; 

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>方式4 </span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>数据类型 数组名[][列数] = { 数据1，数据2 ,数据3，数据4  };</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr4[][<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] = { <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span> };
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：在定义二维数组时，如果初始化了数据，可以省略行数</p>
</blockquote>
<h4><a id="user-content-532-二维数组数组名" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#532-二维数组数组名"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.3.2 二维数组数组名</h4>
<ul>
<li>查看二维数组所占内存空间</li>
<li>获取二维数组首地址</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>二维数组数组名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>][<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] =
	{
		{<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>},
		{<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span>}
	};

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组大小： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组一行大小： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组元素大小： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组行数： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr) / <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组列数： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) / <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>地址</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组首地址：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组第一行地址：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组第二行地址：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组第一个元素地址：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; &amp;arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>二维数组第二个元素地址：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; &amp;arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>][<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结1：二维数组名就是这个数组的首地址</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结2：对二维数组名进行sizeof时，可以获取整个二维数组占用的内存空间大小</p>
</blockquote>
<h4><a id="user-content-533-二维数组应用案例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#533-二维数组应用案例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><strong>5.3.3 二维数组应用案例</strong></h4>
<p><strong>考试成绩统计：</strong></p>
<p>案例描述：有三名同学（张三，李四，王五），在一次考试中的成绩分别如下表，<strong>请分别输出三名同学的总成绩</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th></th>
<th>语文</th>
<th>数学</th>
<th>英语</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>张三</td>
<td>100</td>
<td>100</td>
<td>100</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>李四</td>
<td>90</td>
<td>50</td>
<td>100</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>王五</td>
<td>60</td>
<td>70</td>
<td>80</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>参考答案：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> scores[<span class="pl-c1">3</span>][<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] =
	{
		{<span class="pl-c1">100</span>,<span class="pl-c1">100</span>,<span class="pl-c1">100</span>},
		{<span class="pl-c1">90</span>,<span class="pl-c1">50</span>,<span class="pl-c1">100</span>},
		{<span class="pl-c1">60</span>,<span class="pl-c1">70</span>,<span class="pl-c1">80</span>},
	};

	string names[<span class="pl-c1">3</span>] = { <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>李四<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>王五<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> };

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">3</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">int</span> sum = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">3</span>; j++)
		{
			sum += scores[i][j];
		}
		cout &lt;&lt; names[i] &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>同学总成绩为： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; sum &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-6-函数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#6-函数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6 函数</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-61-概述" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#61-概述"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.1 概述</h3>
<p>**作用：**将一段经常使用的代码封装起来，减少重复代码</p>
<p>一个较大的程序，一般分为若干个程序块，每个模块实现特定的功能。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-62-函数的定义" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#62-函数的定义"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.2 函数的定义</h3>
<p>函数的定义一般主要有5个步骤：</p>
<p>1、返回值类型</p>
<p>2、函数名</p>
<p>3、参数表列</p>
<p>4、函数体语句</p>
<p>5、return 表达式</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>返回值类型 函数名 （参数列表）
{

       函数体语句

       <span class="pl-k">return</span>表达式

}</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>返回值类型 ：一个函数可以返回一个值。在函数定义中</li>
<li>函数名：给函数起个名称</li>
<li>参数列表：使用该函数时，传入的数据</li>
<li>函数体语句：花括号内的代码，函数内需要执行的语句</li>
<li>return表达式： 和返回值类型挂钩，函数执行完后，返回相应的数据</li>
</ul>
<p>**示例：**定义一个加法函数，实现两个数相加</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>函数定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">add</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> num1, <span class="pl-k">int</span> num2)
{
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> sum = num1 + num2;
	<span class="pl-k">return</span> sum;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-63-函数的调用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#63-函数的调用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.3 函数的调用</h3>
<p>**功能：**使用定义好的函数</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code> 函数名（参数）</code></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>函数定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">add</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> num1, <span class="pl-k">int</span> num2) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>定义中的num1,num2称为形式参数，简称形参</span>
{
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> sum = num1 + num2;
	<span class="pl-k">return</span> sum;
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>调用add函数</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> sum = <span class="pl-c1">add</span>(a, b);<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>调用时的a，b称为实际参数，简称实参</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>sum = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; sum &lt;&lt; endl;

	a = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
	b = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;

	sum = <span class="pl-c1">add</span>(a, b);
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>sum = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; sum &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：函数定义里小括号内称为形参，函数调用时传入的参数称为实参</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-64-值传递" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#64-值传递"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.4 值传递</h3>
<ul>
<li>所谓值传递，就是函数调用时实参将数值传入给形参</li>
<li>值传递时，==如果形参发生，并不会影响实参==</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">swap</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> num1, <span class="pl-k">int</span> num2)
{
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>交换前：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>num1 = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; num1 &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>num2 = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; num2 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> temp = num1;
	num1 = num2;
	num2 = temp;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>交换后：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>num1 = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; num1 &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>num2 = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; num2 &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>return ; 当函数声明时候，不需要返回值，可以不写return</span>
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">20</span>;

	<span class="pl-c1">swap</span>(a, b);

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mian中的 a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mian中的 b = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结： 值传递时，形参是修饰不了实参的</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-65-函数的常见样式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#65-函数的常见样式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><strong>6.5 函数的常见样式</strong></h3>
<p>常见的函数样式有4种</p>
<ol>
<li>无参无返</li>
<li>有参无返</li>
<li>无参有返</li>
<li>有参有返</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>函数常见样式</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>1、 无参无返</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">test01</span>()
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>void a = 10; //无类型不可以创建变量,原因无法分配内存</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>this is test01<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>test01(); 函数调用</span>
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>2、 有参无返</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">test02</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a)
{
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>this is test02<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>3、无参有返</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">test03</span>()
{
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>this is test03 <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>4、有参有返</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">test04</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a, <span class="pl-k">int</span> b)
{
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>this is test04 <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> sum = a + b;
	<span class="pl-k">return</span> sum;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-66-函数的声明" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#66-函数的声明"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.6 函数的声明</h3>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 告诉编译器函数名称及如何调用函数。函数的实际主体可以单独定义。</p>
<ul>
<li>函数的<strong>声明可以多次</strong>，但是函数的<strong>定义只能有一次</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>声明可以多次，定义只能一次</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>声明</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">max</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a, <span class="pl-k">int</span> b);
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">max</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a, <span class="pl-k">int</span> b);
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">max</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a, <span class="pl-k">int</span> b)
{
	<span class="pl-k">return</span> a &gt; b ? a : b;
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">200</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-c1">max</span>(a, b) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-67-函数的分文件编写" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#67-函数的分文件编写"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.7 函数的分文件编写</h3>
<p>**作用：**让代码结构更加清晰</p>
<p>函数分文件编写一般有4个步骤</p>
<ol>
<li>创建后缀名为.h的头文件</li>
<li>创建后缀名为.cpp的源文件</li>
<li>在头文件中写函数的声明</li>
<li>在源文件中写函数的定义</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>swap.h文件</span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>实现两个数字交换的函数声明</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">swap</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a, <span class="pl-k">int</span> b);
</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>swap.cpp文件</span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>swap.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">swap</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a, <span class="pl-k">int</span> b)
{
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> temp = a;
	a = b;
	b = temp;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>b = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; endl;
}</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>main函数文件</span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>swap.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">200</span>;
	<span class="pl-c1">swap</span>(a, b);

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}
</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-7-指针" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#7-指针"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7 指针</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-71-指针的基本概念" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#71-指针的基本概念"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.1 指针的基本概念</h3>
<p><strong>指针的作用：</strong> 可以通过指针间接访问内存</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>内存编号是从0开始记录的，一般用十六进制数字表示</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>可以利用指针变量保存地址</p>
<p>​</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-72-指针变量的定义和使用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#72-指针变量的定义和使用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.2 指针变量的定义和使用</h3>
<p>指针变量定义语法： <code>数据类型 * 变量名；</code></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>1、指针的定义</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>定义整型变量a</span>
	
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针定义语法： 数据类型 * 变量名 ;</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> * p;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针变量赋值</span>
	p = &amp;a; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针指向变量a的地址</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; &amp;a &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>打印数据a的地址</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; p &lt;&lt; endl;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>打印指针变量p</span>

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>2、指针的使用</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>通过*操作指针变量指向的内存</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>*p = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; *p &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p>指针变量和普通变量的区别</p>
<ul>
<li>普通变量存放的是数据,指针变量存放的是地址</li>
<li>指针变量可以通过" * "操作符，操作指针变量指向的内存空间，这个过程称为解引用</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>总结1： 我们可以通过 &amp; 符号 获取变量的地址</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结2：利用指针可以记录地址</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结3：对指针变量解引用，可以操作指针指向的内存</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-73-指针所占内存空间" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#73-指针所占内存空间"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.3 指针所占内存空间</h3>
<p>提问：指针也是种数据类型，那么这种数据类型占用多少内存空间？</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> * p;
	p = &amp;a; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针指向数据a的地址</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; *p &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>* 解引用</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(p) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">char</span> *) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">float</span> *) &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">double</span> *) &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：所有指针类型在32位操作系统下是4个字节</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-74-空指针和野指针" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#74-空指针和野指针"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.4 空指针和野指针</h3>
<p><strong>空指针</strong>：指针变量指向内存中编号为0的空间</p>
<p>**用途：**初始化指针变量</p>
<p>**注意：**空指针指向的内存是不可以访问的</p>
<p><strong>示例1：空指针</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针变量p指向内存地址编号为0的空间</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> * p = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>访问空指针报错 </span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>内存编号0 ~255为系统占用内存，不允许用户访问</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; *p &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p><strong>野指针</strong>：指针变量指向非法的内存空间</p>
<p><strong>示例2：野指针</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针变量p指向内存地址编号为0x1100的空间</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> * p = (<span class="pl-k">int</span> *)<span class="pl-c1">0x1100</span>;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>访问野指针报错 </span>
	cout &lt;&lt; *p &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：空指针和野指针都不是我们申请的空间，因此不要访问。</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-75-const修饰指针" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#75-const修饰指针"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.5 const修饰指针</h3>
<p>const修饰指针有三种情况</p>
<ol>
<li>const修饰指针   --- 常量指针</li>
<li>const修饰常量   --- 指针常量</li>
<li>const即修饰指针，又修饰常量</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>const修饰的是指针，指针指向可以改，指针指向的值不可以更改</span>
	<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span> * p1 = &amp;a; 
	p1 = &amp;b; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>正确</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>*p1 = 100;  报错</span>
	

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>const修饰的是常量，指针指向不可以改，指针指向的值可以更改</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> * <span class="pl-k">const</span> p2 = &amp;a;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>p2 = &amp;b; //错误</span>
	*p2 = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>正确</span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>const既修饰指针又修饰常量</span>
	<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span> * <span class="pl-k">const</span> p3 = &amp;a;
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>p3 = &amp;b; //错误</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>*p3 = 100; //错误</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>技巧：看const右侧紧跟着的是指针还是常量, 是指针就是常量指针，是常量就是指针常量</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-76-指针和数组" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#76-指针和数组"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.6 指针和数组</h3>
<p>**作用：**利用指针访问数组中元素</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[] = { <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span>,<span class="pl-c1">7</span>,<span class="pl-c1">8</span>,<span class="pl-c1">9</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span> };

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> * p = arr;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指向数组的指针</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>第一个元素： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] &lt;&lt; endl;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>指针访问第一个元素： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; *p &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>利用指针遍历数组</span>
		cout &lt;&lt; *p &lt;&lt; endl;
		p++;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-77-指针和函数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#77-指针和函数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.7 指针和函数</h3>
<p>**作用：**利用指针作函数参数，可以修改实参的值</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>值传递</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">swap1</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> a ,<span class="pl-k">int</span> b)
{
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> temp = a;
	a = b; 
	b = temp;
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>地址传递</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">swap2</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> * p1, <span class="pl-k">int</span> *p2)
{
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> temp = *p1;
	*p1 = *p2;
	*p2 = temp;
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> a = <span class="pl-c1">10</span>;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> b = <span class="pl-c1">20</span>;
	<span class="pl-c1">swap1</span>(a, b); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 值传递不会改变实参</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">swap2</span>(&amp;a, &amp;b); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>地址传递会改变实参</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>a = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; a &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>b = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; b &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：如果不想修改实参，就用值传递，如果想修改实参，就用地址传递</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-78-指针数组函数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#78-指针数组函数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.8 指针、数组、函数</h3>
<p>**案例描述：**封装一个函数，利用冒泡排序，实现对整型数组的升序排序</p>
<p>例如数组：int arr[10] = { 4,3,6,9,1,2,10,8,7,5 };</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>冒泡排序函数</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">bubbleSort</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> * arr, <span class="pl-k">int</span> len)  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>int * arr 也可以写为int arr[]</span>
{
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; len - <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; len - <span class="pl-c1">1</span> - i; j++)
		{
			<span class="pl-k">if</span> (arr[j] &gt; arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>])
			{
				<span class="pl-k">int</span> temp = arr[j];
				arr[j] = arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>];
				arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>] = temp;
			}
		}
	}
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>打印数组函数</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">printArray</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[], <span class="pl-k">int</span> len)
{
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; len; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; arr[i] &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">10</span>] = { <span class="pl-c1">4</span>,<span class="pl-c1">3</span>,<span class="pl-c1">6</span>,<span class="pl-c1">9</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span>,<span class="pl-c1">8</span>,<span class="pl-c1">7</span>,<span class="pl-c1">5</span> };
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> len = <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr) / <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span>);

	<span class="pl-c1">bubbleSort</span>(arr, len);

	<span class="pl-c1">printArray</span>(arr, len);

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：当数组名传入到函数作为参数时，被退化为指向首元素的指针</p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-8-结构体" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#8-结构体"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8 结构体</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-81-结构体基本概念" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#81-结构体基本概念"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.1 结构体基本概念</h3>
<p>结构体属于用户==自定义的数据类型==，允许用户存储不同的数据类型</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-82-结构体定义和使用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#82-结构体定义和使用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.2 结构体定义和使用</h3>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code>struct 结构体名 { 结构体成员列表 }；</code></p>
<p>通过结构体创建变量的方式有三种：</p>
<ul>
<li>struct 结构体名 变量名</li>
<li>struct 结构体名 变量名 = { 成员1值 ， 成员2值...}</li>
<li>定义结构体时顺便创建变量</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>分数</span>
}stu3; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体变量创建方式3 </span>


<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体变量创建方式1</span>
	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span> stu1; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>struct 关键字可以省略</span>

	stu1.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	stu1.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> = <span class="pl-c1">18</span>;
	stu1.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
	
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu1.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu1.<span class="pl-smi">age</span>  &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu1.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体变量创建方式2</span>
	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span> stu2 = { <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>李四<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">19</span>,<span class="pl-c1">60</span> };

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu2.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu2.<span class="pl-smi">age</span>  &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu2.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;


	stu3.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>王五<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	stu3.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> = <span class="pl-c1">18</span>;
	stu3.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> = <span class="pl-c1">80</span>;
	

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu3.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu3.<span class="pl-smi">age</span>  &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu3.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结1：定义结构体时的关键字是struct，不可省略</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结2：创建结构体变量时，关键字struct可以省略</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>总结3：结构体变量利用操作符 ''.''  访问成员</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-83-结构体数组" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#83-结构体数组"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.3 结构体数组</h3>
<p>**作用：**将自定义的结构体放入到数组中方便维护</p>
<p><strong>语法：</strong><code> struct  结构体名 数组名[元素个数] = {  {} , {} , ... {} }</code></p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>分数</span>
}<span class="pl-ii"></span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体数组</span>
	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">3</span>]=
	{
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">18</span>,<span class="pl-c1">80</span> },
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>李四<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">19</span>,<span class="pl-c1">60</span> },
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>王五<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-c1">70</span> }
	};

	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="pl-c1">3</span>; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[i].<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[i].<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[i].<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-84-结构体指针" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#84-结构体指针"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.4 结构体指针</h3>
<p>**作用：**通过指针访问结构体中的成员</p>
<ul>
<li>利用操作符 <code>-&gt; </code>可以通过结构体指针访问结构体属性</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>分数</span>
};


<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
	
	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span> stu = { <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">18</span>,<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, };
	
	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span> * p = &amp;stu;
	
	p-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">score</span> = <span class="pl-c1">80</span>; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>指针通过 -&gt; 操作符可以访问成员</span>

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; p-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; p-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; p-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：结构体指针可以通过 -&gt; 操作符 来访问结构体中的成员</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-85-结构体嵌套结构体" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#85-结构体嵌套结构体"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.5 结构体嵌套结构体</h3>
<p><strong>作用：</strong> 结构体中的成员可以是另一个结构体</p>
<p>**例如：**每个老师辅导一个学员，一个老师的结构体中，记录一个学生的结构体</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>学生结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>分数</span>
};

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>教师结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">teacher</span>
{
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> id; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>职工编号</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>教师姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>教师年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span> stu; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>子结构体 学生</span>
};


<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">teacher</span> t1;
	t1.<span class="pl-smi">id</span> = <span class="pl-c1">10000</span>;
	t1.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>老王<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	t1.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> = <span class="pl-c1">40</span>;

	t1.<span class="pl-smi">stu</span>.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	t1.<span class="pl-smi">stu</span>.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> = <span class="pl-c1">18</span>;
	t1.<span class="pl-smi">stu</span>.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> = <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;

	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>教师 职工编号： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t1.<span class="pl-smi">id</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 姓名： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t1.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t1.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>辅导学员 姓名： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t1.<span class="pl-smi">stu</span>.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t1.<span class="pl-smi">stu</span>.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 考试分数： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t1.<span class="pl-smi">stu</span>.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p>**总结：**在结构体中可以定义另一个结构体作为成员，用来解决实际问题</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-86-结构体做函数参数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#86-结构体做函数参数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.6 结构体做函数参数</h3>
<p>**作用：**将结构体作为参数向函数中传递</p>
<p>传递方式有两种：</p>
<ul>
<li>值传递</li>
<li>地址传递</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>学生结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>分数</span>
};

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>值传递</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">printStudent</span>(student stu )
{
	stu.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> = <span class="pl-c1">28</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>子函数中 姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">age</span>  &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>地址传递</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">printStudent2</span>(student *stu)
{
	stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">age</span> = <span class="pl-c1">28</span>;
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>子函数中 姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">age</span>  &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	student stu = { <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">18</span>,<span class="pl-c1">100</span>};
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>值传递</span>
	<span class="pl-c1">printStudent</span>(stu);
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>主函数中 姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;

	cout &lt;&lt; endl;

	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>地址传递</span>
	<span class="pl-c1">printStudent2</span>(&amp;stu);
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>主函数中 姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">age</span>  &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu.<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
