	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>总结：如果不想修改主函数中的数据，用值传递，反之用地址传递</p>
</blockquote>
<h3><a id="user-content-87-结构体中-const使用场景" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#87-结构体中-const使用场景"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.7 结构体中 const使用场景</h3>
<p>**作用：**用const来防止误操作</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>学生结构体定义</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">student</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>成员列表</span>
	string name;  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>姓名</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>年龄</span>
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>分数</span>
};

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>const使用场景</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">printStudent</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> student *stu) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>加const防止函数体中的误操作</span>
{
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>stu-&gt;age = 100; //操作失败，因为加了const修饰</span>
	cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; stu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;

}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	student stu = { <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张三<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">18</span>,<span class="pl-c1">100</span> };

	<span class="pl-c1">printStudent</span>(&amp;stu);

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-88-结构体案例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#88-结构体案例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.8 结构体案例</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-881-案例1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#881-案例1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.8.1 案例1</h4>
<p><strong>案例描述：</strong></p>
<p>学校正在做毕设项目，每名老师带领5个学生，总共有3名老师，需求如下</p>
<p>设计学生和老师的结构体，其中在老师的结构体中，有老师姓名和一个存放5名学生的数组作为成员</p>
<p>学生的成员有姓名、考试分数，创建数组存放3名老师，通过函数给每个老师及所带的学生赋值</p>
<p>最终打印出老师数据以及老师所带的学生数据。</p>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">Student</span>
{
	string name;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> score;
};
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">Teacher</span>
{
	string name;
	Student <span class="pl-smi">sArray</span>[<span class="pl-c1">5</span>];
};

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">allocateSpace</span>(Teacher tArray[] , <span class="pl-k">int</span> len)
{
	string tName = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>教师<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	string <span class="pl-smi">sName</span> = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>学生<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	string nameSeed = <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ABCDE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; len; i++)
	{
		tArray[i].<span class="pl-smi">name</span> = tName + nameSeed[i];
		
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">5</span>; j++)
		{
			tArray[i].<span class="pl-smi">sArray</span>[j].<span class="pl-smi">name</span> = <span class="pl-smi">sName</span> + nameSeed[j];
			tArray[i].<span class="pl-smi">sArray</span>[j].<span class="pl-smi">score</span> = <span class="pl-c1">rand</span>() % <span class="pl-c1">61</span> + <span class="pl-c1">40</span>;
		}
	}
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">printTeachers</span>(Teacher tArray[], <span class="pl-k">int</span> len)
{
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; len; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; tArray[i].<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; <span class="pl-c1">5</span>; j++)
		{
			cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\t</span>姓名：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; tArray[i].<span class="pl-smi">sArray</span>[j].<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 分数：<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; tArray[i].<span class="pl-smi">sArray</span>[j].<span class="pl-smi">score</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
		}
	}
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-c1">srand</span>((<span class="pl-k">unsigned</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>)<span class="pl-c1">time</span>(<span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>)); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>随机数种子 头文件 #include &lt;ctime&gt;</span>

	Teacher tArray[<span class="pl-c1">3</span>]; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>老师数组</span>

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> len = <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(tArray) / <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(Teacher);

	<span class="pl-c1">allocateSpace</span>(tArray, len); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>创建数据</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">printTeachers</span>(tArray, len); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>打印数据</span>
	
	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-882-案例2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#882-案例2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.8.2 案例2</h4>
<p><strong>案例描述：</strong></p>
<p>设计一个英雄的结构体，包括成员姓名，年龄，性别;创建结构体数组，数组中存放5名英雄。</p>
<p>通过冒泡排序的算法，将数组中的英雄按照年龄进行升序排序，最终打印排序后的结果。</p>
<p>五名英雄信息如下：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>刘备<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">23</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>关羽<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">22</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张飞<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>赵云<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">21</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>貂蝉<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">19</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>女<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},</pre></div>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>英雄结构体</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">hero</span>
{
	string name;
	<span class="pl-k">int</span> age;
	string sex;
};
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>冒泡排序</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">bubbleSort</span>(hero arr[] , <span class="pl-k">int</span> len)
{
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; len - <span class="pl-c1">1</span>; i++)
	{
		<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; len - <span class="pl-c1">1</span> - i; j++)
		{
			<span class="pl-k">if</span> (arr[j].<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &gt; arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>].<span class="pl-smi">age</span>)
			{
				hero temp = arr[j];
				arr[j] = arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>];
				arr[j + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>] = temp;
			}
		}
	}
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>打印数组</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">printHeros</span>(hero arr[], <span class="pl-k">int</span> len)
{
	<span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> i = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; i &lt; len; i++)
	{
		cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>姓名： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[i].<span class="pl-smi">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 性别： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[i].<span class="pl-smi">sex</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> 年龄： <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; arr[i].<span class="pl-smi">age</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
	}
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {

	<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">hero</span> arr[<span class="pl-c1">5</span>] =
	{
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>刘备<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">23</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>关羽<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">22</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>张飞<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>赵云<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">21</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>男<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
		{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>貂蝉<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-c1">19</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>女<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>},
	};

	<span class="pl-k">int</span> len = <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(arr) / <span class="pl-k">sizeof</span>(hero); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>获取数组元素个数</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">bubbleSort</span>(arr, len); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>排序</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">printHeros</span>(arr, len); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>打印</span>

	<span class="pl-c1">system</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pause<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

	<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
